Important News

Cheng Zhiyuan 86

Massacring Righteous Troops in Heilongjiang

▲Zhang Wenzhu Aids Tyranny

▲Li Chengzhang Curses Traitors

▲Cheng Zhiyuan Sacrifices Railroads

A dispatch from Beiping reveals information from individuals from Heilongjiang. Since Cheng Zhiyuan assumed the position of puppet governor, he has not only been willing to serve as a puppet for the Japanese, harming people with ambition, but also revealing all of Marshal Ma's previous plans. His accomplice in aiding tyranny is the puppet Chief of Staff, Zhang Wenzhu. All insidious schemes pass through Zhang's hands, and he is now favored by the Japanese and Cheng, the traitor. Zhang, whose courtesy name is Dingyuan, is thirty-six years old, from Wuxi County, Sichuan Province, and a graduate of the Baoding Military Academy. He rose from company commander and aide-de-camp to staff officer. In the fourteenth year of the Republic [1925], when Ma Zhanshan was the commander of the Fourth Mixed Brigade of Heilongjiang, he promoted Zhang to be the Chief of Staff of that Brigade. Later, when Ma Zhanshan was promoted to the commander of the Seventeenth Division, he appointed Zhang as the Chief of Staff of the Seventeenth Division. When Wan Fulin was the Military Governor of Jiang, with Ma's support, he was appointed as the commander of the Second Regiment of the Cavalry First Brigade. Having received such favor from Ma, he has now lost his conscience and betrayed his principles, a truly lamentable example of human ingratitude. According to a person from Zhaodong County, after Cheng and Zhang harmed Marshal Ma's associates, the Japanese have placed exceptional trust in them. Cheng and Zhang are overjoyed and beside themselves with delight. Recently, translated copies of Marshal Ma's secret telegrams, such as the Jiang secret, the Kui secret, the Vice secret, and the Military secret telegrams, have been handed over to the Japanese. The Japanese have already reprinted many copies of these telegrams and distributed them to various locations to intercept news from various places. Currently, the people of all counties in Jiang Province are extremely indignant towards the Japanese and Cheng and Zhang, and have formed Red Spear Societies and Big Sword Teams for self-defense. The Japanese, recognizing the urgency of the situation, have telegraphed Japan, requesting the immediate dispatch of a large army to Heilongjiang. They have also ordered Cheng Zhiyuan to quickly form two cavalry detachments to attack anti-Japanese elements. On June 1st, Cheng Zhiyuan appointed Zhang Wenzhu as the commander of the First Cavalry Detachment, Jia Jinming as the commander of the Second Cavalry Detachment, and Zhou Zuolin as the Bandit Suppression督战 Commander, and together with the entire 16th Regiment of the Japanese 15th Brigade, they departed for the Zhaodong area to attack Li Haiqing's army. Zhang Wenzhu dispatched the Third Battalion Commander Tong Yuheng of the Second Brigade's supplementary regiment (Wang Shutang's unit) leading over three hundred soldiers, to launch a brave and fierce attack. Li Haiqing used eight thousand cavalry to surround and attack them. Tong's soldiers were at a loss, some surrendering and some fleeing. The puppet military officers were all executed by Li's army. The Japanese army, blaming Tong's battalion for its defeat, severely reprimanded Zhang Wenzhu and others for their ineffective combat and gave them two days to retake Zhaodong. At that time, Li Haiqing's army, stationed in the city, numbered approximately eight thousand men, deployed for defense. Zhang, under the order of the Japanese army, urgently督促團 (Quan Sheng), 祝團 (Feng Yang), 檀團 (Zi Xin), 霍團 and other regiments to attack with all their might. The intensity of the artillery fire was unprecedented. Li's army, lacking artillery, had the north gate of the county town broken by the 凃團 and captured the 烧锅 and county government office. Li's army attacked from outside the courtyard. The 凃團 defended to the death without coming out. Li's army then bored holes in the residential houses to use as gunports and aimed their guns. When the 凃團 lacked water and went out to fetch it, Li's army shot and killed them. Beside the well outside the east wall of the county government office alone, there were over a hundred corpses. The 凃團, lacking sufficient water, then desperately attacked to the death. The two sides then engaged in street fighting. Due to the excessive number of people, the streets were crowded, and countless civilians were killed in the chaos. The Japanese army then used eight airplanes, flying low, to drop bombs continuously, along with five armored vehicles, using machine guns to strafe Li's army. The bullets fell like rain, and more than ten field guns fired in continuous volleys. Where the airplanes went, the artillery followed. The houses in the city collapsed, and the people were left with broken arms and legs. Li's army, unable to withstand the fierce destruction, retreated to the Fengle Township area. After the county town was occupied, the search for Li's troops was extremely strict. Currently, spring plowing in the Zhaodong and Zhaozhou areas is completely hopeless, and many people are displaced. Zhang Wenzhu captured Li Chengzhang, the Chief of Staff and Director of Finance of Li's army (also known as Li Dianwen), and sent him to the provincial capital on the 16th. Cheng, the traitor, personally interrogated him. Li Chengzhang loudly cursed Cheng's shamelessness and madness. Cheng then sentenced Li to death. On the day before the execution, he sent letters to the Japanese Consulate, the South Manchuria Railway Company, the Special Service Agency, and the Japanese Army Headquarters, inviting them to send people to attend the event. The Japanese temporarily notified the Public Security Bureau to prepare four hundred vehicles for their use. On that day, the crowd of spectators was immense. It was one o'clock in the afternoon on June 17th. Li was taken from the Army Prison and tied to the West Great Bridge for execution by shooting. Li's expression did not change, and he described his purpose in joining the righteous army, saying, ("I am neither a bandit nor a thief. I am a true Chinese and cannot bear to see our territory fall to foreign races. To wipe away the nickname of 'slaves of a fallen nation' for our people, I joined the volunteer army. I am willing to die so that the Wokou know that the hearts of our people have not died, and the Chinese nation can never be subdued by the pressure of power. My death is for the Republic of China. I hope my compatriots will become angrier with each setback and continue to strive.")

When Li saw that the executioner was Wang Shutang, the commander of the supplementary regiment, he shouted, ("Wang Shutang, Zhang Wenzhu, Cheng Zhiyuan, you are also serving your country, but I cannot say which country you are serving!") After the execution, all the spectators shed tears, but the execution soldiers, on their way back to camp, still loudly sang the military song ("The Yellow race should enjoy the Yellow Sea rights, Asians should cultivate Asian fields, youths, youths, do not engage in fratricide"), revealing the ignorance of the soldiers.

On June 16th, Cheng Zhiyuan appointed the Japanese Niwakawa as the Director of the Police Department and Inada Ichiro as the Director of the General Affairs Department. It is reported that the Japanese have finalized a plan to resettle veterans in the Northeast, confiscating uncultivated wasteland and evicting tenant farmers from their land for the veterans to cultivate, with every hundred families forming a village. They have already sent people to various places to investigate soil quality and products, and it is planned to temporarily move 50,000 veteran households to Heilongjiang this year.

The Qiqihar-Keshan Railway Bureau was terminated on June 15th and taken over by the Tao'an-Ang'angxi Railway Bureau. The Japanese have recruited 3,000 workers to work day and night to expedite the construction of the section from Aolonggou to Keshan on the Qiqihar-Keshan Railway. It is scheduled that the section from Aolonggou via Keshan to Kedong County will be connected to the Qiqihar-Hailun Railway by September 1st. The Japanese are actively repairing the section from Laha Station to Nehe on the Qiqihar-Keshan Railway, which is ninety li long, for the convenience of military movements. It is scheduled to be completed this month.

On June 17th, Cheng, the traitor, executed a Marshal Ma's regiment commander Li Rong. On June 18th, the Japanese army dispatched the Koizumi Detachment to attack Ma's army in the direction of Nehe. Ma's army's Xu Zihe Brigade has already retreated from Nehe to Nenjiang. According to a person from Keshan County, it was captured by the Red Spear Society on June 20th. Over twenty Japanese soldiers were killed or wounded, and they soon withdrew. The county magistrate and the director of the Public Security Bureau have both disappeared. Currently, the Japanese army is demanding one hundred horse-drawn carriages from each county, and the people cannot afford to supply them and are fleeing. Those with guns and youths, unable to withstand the various oppressions of bandits, are secretly planning to risk their lives. No one is cultivating the fields more than ten li outside the city in each county. There are concerns that there will be a grain shortage after the autumn harvest. Bandits are everywhere in the counties, bandits and soldiers are indistinguishable, and the old, the young, men, and women are helpless and fleeing in all directions. The Nenjiang River has overflowed and flooded over a thousand villages and towns. The scale of the flood has not been seen in nearly thirty years. Between natural disasters and human calamities, the people truly do not know where their death will be. (July 7th)

Hebei Provincial Government Report 87

Tragedy at Baoding Second Normal School

▲Students Refuse to Accept Takeover, Leading to Conflict

▲Resulting in Six Student Deaths and Five Injuries

▲Baoding Area Now Under Martial Law

A dispatch from Tianjin states that the communist dispute at the Provincial Baoding Second Normal School has dragged on for many days without resolution. The Provincial Government, fearing further complications, telegraphed Ji Yuan County Magistrate Jing Jinliang and Baoding Public Security Bureau Director Li Enpei, ordering them to take over the school, with the county to manage the school's assets and temporarily close it until it could be reorganized and reopened. Unexpectedly, the Baoding garrison and the Public Security Bureau went to take over the school on the morning of the 5th, resulting in a conflict with the students, leading to six student deaths, five injuries, and thirty-eight arrests. Due to the seriousness of the matter, the Provincial Government convened the press on the 7th to report the incident and requested careful reporting. The details are as follows: The Department of Education believed that the Second Normal School's student unrest had taken on a political character, going beyond the scope of purely educational administration, and therefore submitted a proposal to the Provincial Government to resolve the issue, requesting the Provincial Government to handle it. The resolution was approved. The original proposal stated: "The Second Normal School students are occupying the school and resisting reorganization. We submit a proposal for handling it for public decision." Regarding the proposal: Upon investigation, it was found that the Baoding Second Normal School was involved in a communist dispute, and an order was given to investigate and deal with the matter. The school was first closed for a vacation for reorganization, and a reorganization proposal was submitted to the meeting. It was resolved to approve the measures proposed by the Department and strictly handle the matter according to the law, and reports were to be made. After receiving the order, Qingyuan County Magistrate Jin and Baoding Public Security Bureau Director Li were telegraphed on June 13th, stating that since the reorganization of the case had been resolved by the Provincial Government, all students were prohibited from entering the school before being summoned, and personnel were sent to take over the school. It was then reported that the Second Normal School students had defied the Department's order on the 15th of this month, illegally entered the school, and the situation was serious and impossible to take over. The Provincial Government also telegraphed the garrison in Baoding, requesting assistance in handling the matter. The Department also repeatedly telegraphed the political and police organs in Baoding, requesting strict precautions and joint action to quickly conclude the matter and carry out the reorganization. However, the students remained obstinate and occupied the school, resisting takeover. Members of the Department reported that the students had tightly closed the school gates, patrolled the school walls with guns, had bricks and tiles prepared, and did not allow civilians to enter, and they also occupied neighboring houses, demolishing two of them. On the evening of June 23rd, during a rainstorm, more than twenty people rushed out, each carrying knives and guns, and purchased ten bags of flour in the vicinity of the school. Furthermore, according to Baoding Public Security Bureau Director Li Enhou and Qingyuan County Magistrate Jin Liangji, they reported that they had received the urgent telegrams and that the Director and Magistrate had repeatedly and earnestly persuaded the students to no avail. In accordance with the telegrams of the Provincial Department, they consulted with the commander of the 14th Brigade of the Army to determine a困 method to soften them. Since June 23rd, over a hundred soldiers and police officers had been dispatched to surround the school, and the electricity and telephone lines were cut off to stop their news and cut off their communication. The students returned to the school and took advantage of the unpreparedness of the soldiers and police officers to break out twenty people to buy ten bags of flour into the school. It was estimated that with this supply, they could last another ten days, and the students were sending out declarations and arbitrarily scolding the outside, and they had stored many knives, guns, clubs, bricks, and stones to resist. Judging by their actions, it was not comparable to ordinary student unrest. The Director and Magistrate were deeply afraid of being too hasty and causing damage, so they delayed and failed to act quickly. Before receiving the telegram, they reported the reason and consulted closely with Commander Chen, believing that such a delay was not a solution. If force were used to expel them, a solution could be achieved quickly, but after examining the situation, it was determined that the students would resist, and once started, damage to both sides was inevitable. They hesitated again and again and dared not act rashly. They respectfully submitted the actual situation and requested investigation and approval on how to resolve the matter in order to follow. While reviewing the matter, the Department's members, Wang Jin et al., telegraphed, "The telegram has been received. After contacting the County Bureau, it was said that they had telegraphed the Fu and Ting to request instructions. Unexpectedly, during this period, the students in the school robbed ten bags of flour and two bags of white rice, and their arrogance was greater than before. It was heard that the stolen items were supplied by someone, and it was heard that there was indeed an organization of students outside the school. If it is not resolved early, the dispute may expand." According to these circumstances, it was found that the communist party was rampant in the school before, and the Department had a reorganization plan. Later, they received an order to strictly handle the matter, and personnel were repeatedly sent to handle it carefully. It was originally hoped that the reorganization would be completed in the shortest time, so a vacation was first granted to consider the students' departure and retention. At that time, only two students in the school were sick and had not left. After leaving the school, they re-entered the school, and after being surrounded, they were able to enter and exit, so that the students always resisted and refused to accept the takeover. Such gathering of people to resist orders is truly ignoring the law and discipline and cannot be tolerated again. It is proposed to dissolve the school and temporarily close it, and to adopt the measures of closing the Baoding Second Vocational School. All public property and official documents are to be received and kept by the Baoding Public Security Bureau Qingyuan County to facilitate cleaning. After the cleaning is completed in the future, it will be reopened. If this plan is adopted, please telegraph the Baoding Public Security Bureau Qingyuan County to handle it properly. Is this appropriate? It is proposed for public decision and implementation." Member and Director of the Department of Education Chen Baoquan, after the resolution of this case was approved, the Provincial Government immediately telegraphed the Baoding Public Security Bureau Director and the Qingyuan County Magistrate, ordering them to comply, with the general meaning being to strictly arrest the ringleaders, dissolve the coerced, and consider the severity of the situation to deal with it accordingly. However, when taking over the school, if the students resisted, they were only allowed to use wooden sticks and martial arts and were not allowed to open fire. After the Baoding Public Security Bureau Director and the Qingyuan County Magistrate telegraphed, they discussed the takeover measures and decided to dispatch soldiers of a 旅 長,派旅長陈部队 and police of a大队 from the保安队 to take over. On the night of the 5th, they had once consulted with the party headquarters, the Education Bureau, and the students' parents to persuade the students to leave the school, but to no avail. There was only one way to take over by force. At三时 in the前夜, they used撓鉤, 鐵叉 to dig open a corner of the school, and the soldiers and police officers poured in. The students were prepared and resisted with weapons. First, several shots were fired, followed by a dense fire of large guns, totaling over a hundred shots, which lasted for an hour before stopping. After investigation, six or seven students died from gunshot wounds, five were seriously injured, one student's right leg was blown off, his knee was炸裂, and it had to be sawed off. One student had a gunshot wound to the chest and his intestines were exposed, one student had a stab wound to the chest, and the remaining two students were injured in the legs. All were taken to Si Luo Hospital. The hospital, being charitable in nature, immediately performed emergency surgery. The blood was flowing, and the situation was extremely tragic. The remaining thirty-eight students were arrested, escorted into the city by soldiers and police officers, and detained in the playground of the Second Model Elementary School. At seven o'clock in the morning on the 6th, military police, political figures, sleeves, brigade commanders, public security bureau directors, county magistrates, etc., all went to the school by rickshaw to investigate. They then inspected the soldiers and police officers under their command, who were all unharmed. All the parents were panic-stricken and in a state of great pain, rushing to the school to inquire. Furthermore, according to relevant sources, they received a report stating that many communists were lurking in the Baoding Second Normal School, wantonly luring young people and inciting unrest. Recently, the authorities in Beijing and Ping have received numerous reports that the communist bandits were hiding weapons in the school, intending to start an uprising in Baoding, using the Second Normal School as a base for launching the uprising. Therefore, they issued an order to dissolve the school to prevent the situation from escalating. Unexpectedly, the students of the school were incited by the communist bandits, tightly closed the gates, and confronted the soldiers and police officers. The two sides were in a standoff for four days. This morning (the 7th), at around nine o'clock, dozens of gunshots were suddenly heard from the rear wall of the school. While the soldiers and police officers stationed outside the school were surprised, they saw many bandits lying on the school walls, shooting outwards with box cannons and handguns. The soldiers and police officers were caught off guard and immediately one person was killed and seven or eight were injured. At this point, the soldiers and police officers also opened fire in retaliation, intending to forcibly enter the school and search for the communist bandits. Unexpectedly, the communist bandits mixed in with the student ranks, rushed out with guns, and stabbed the soldiers and police officers with knives and kitchen knives. The soldiers and police officers also fought back with bayonets. In this melee, a total of six young men were killed by the soldiers and police officers, and five or six were also injured. The school authorities are currently identifying the bodies. It is said that most of the dead were ultra-leftist elements who had recently come to study. As for the soldiers and police officers, as of the time of the report, four had died and twelve were injured. Martial law has now been declared in the Baoding area. (7th)

Hunan Province Establishes 88

Military Expenditure Reorganization Committee

▲Specifies Monthly Military Expenditure Amount to be Paid by National Tax Agencies

▲Minimum Amount is 1.2 Million Yuan

A dispatch from Changsha states that the Fourth Route Army's military expenditures have been traditionally covered by Hunan Province's national tax revenue. Since the occurrence of banditry and floods last year, tax revenue has decreased, and military expenditures have been in arrears for five months (only food has been issued, and officers and soldiers have not been paid). This year, austerity measures have been strictly enforced, and payments have been issued at 50%, 60%, and 80% of the original amount, with monthly dual fees reduced to 1.2 million yuan. However, due to the shortfalls in salt tax and the lack of special tax revenue, the military expenditure for June has not been fully paid, and the food for July is not secured. He Jian now believes that it is at a time when the suppression of bandits is tense and funds are urgently needed. If measures are not taken to reorganize and enrich the source of funds, it will be difficult to maintain the situation. Therefore, the day before, he convened the managers of various divisions and the heads of national tax and financial agencies to discuss rescue measures and decided to establish a Military Expenditure Reorganization Committee to bring together managers of various divisions and heads of national tax agencies to jointly discuss reorganization and enrichment methods. At that time, eleven articles of organization regulations were drafted, and He Jian appointed Huang Weihan, Ling Zhang, Tai Shiding, Wang Han, Xie Qi, He Zhiwen, Liu Yunsheng, Chen Qingguang, Hu Zhaoyuan, Yi Fengteng, Yang Daguan, Zhang Ganqun, Gui Runsong, Jiang Guozhang, Huang Huiseng, Li Yi, Zhang Yuzhou, Wang Jiading, Chen Rujin, Wang Shijian, Tang Zanyu, Xie Jizhen, and Chen Gubang as members, and appointed Liu Yinggu as the chairman of the committee. The inaugural meeting was held at the Fourth Route Army headquarters on July 8th, and the committee stipulated the amount of military expenditure that each national tax agency should pay each month. The Customs Transportation Bureau and the Audit Office should pay 900,000 yuan per month, the Tobacco and Alcohol Stamp Bureau should pay 90,000 yuan per month, the Cigarette and Kerosene Special Tax should pay 60,000 yuan per month, and the Special Tax Office should pay 150,000 yuan per month, totaling 1.2 million yuan as the minimum amount. If there is a large amount of special tax revenue, it will be used to clear arrears. However, in any case, 1.2 million yuan must be paid each month according to the above ratio, so that there will be no shortage of salaries in the future. The regulations of the Military Expenditure Reorganization Committee are recorded as follows: (Article 1) This Route Army has specially established the Military Expenditure Reorganization Committee in order to enrich military expenditures and ensure the authenticity and transparency of income and expenditure. (Article 2) The members of this committee are organized by the following personnel: 1. Chief of Staff, Chiefs of various departments, and section chiefs of the Management Department of the Headquarters. 2. Chiefs of the Management Departments of each division. 3. Director of the Xiang'an Customs Transportation Bureau. 4. Director of the Xiang'an Salt Affairs Audit Office. 5. Director of the Hunan Special Tax Clearing Office. 6. Director of the Supervision Office. 7. Director of the Hunan Stamp Tobacco and Alcohol Tax Bureau. 8. Special Commissioners of the Commander-in-Chief and other personnel handling special tax affairs. The Chief of Staff shall be the Chairman of the Committee, and the Chief of the Management Department shall act as the Chairman when he is absent due to work. (Article 3) This committee is responsible for supervising, assessing, planning, and reorganizing the income and expenditure of the military expenditure of this Route Army based on the following principles: (1) The expenditure of the military expenditure of this Route Army must strictly adhere to the budget. Except for the necessary temporary expenses approved and issued by the Commander-in-Chief, if there is any payment exceeding 500 yuan outside the budget, it must be submitted to this committee for review before payment can be made. (2) This Route Army

Achieve the purpose of enriching. (Article 4) In order to clarify the income and expenditure situation, each tax revenue agency and the Management Department shall submit a report of the income and expenditure of funds to the meeting three days before the meeting each month. (Article 5) The resolutions of this meeting shall be submitted to the Commander-in-Chief for approval at any time and issued to be implemented separately. (Article 6) This committee shall hold a regular meeting once a month, the meeting period is the 10th of each month, but when the Commander-in-Chief submits a proposal for deliberation, and the Chairman deems it necessary or upon request of more than three members, a temporary meeting may also be convened. (Article 7) The proposals of each member of this meeting shall be submitted to the meeting three days before the meeting and included in the agenda. (Article 8) This meeting shall not be opened unless more than half of the members are present, and no resolution shall be adopted unless more than half of the members present agree. If the number of votes for and against is equal, the Chairman may submit the matter to the Commander-in-Chief for approval. (Article 9) Each member shall not be absent from the meeting at will. If it is necessary to be absent due to necessary matters, they shall also entrust a corresponding person to attend on their behalf. (Article 10) If there are any matters not covered in these regulations, they may be amended at any time. (Article 11) These regulations shall be implemented from the date of promulgation.

Shandong Province Continues to Issue One Million Jiao Notes 89

A dispatch from Jinan states that various counties in this province were previously flooded with paper money, with no restrictions. After the Provincial Government strictly banned them, they were completely prohibited. Since the establishment of the Ping 市 Official Money Bureau, 500,000 yuan of 角 Notes have been issued to facilitate the circulation of people's trade (200,000 yuan circulated in Jinan, Weixian, Jining, Tengxian, and Linqing, 160,000 yuan circulated, and 140,000 yuan circulated in Qingdao, Yantai, Longkou, Zhoucun, Boshan, and Tai'an). For more than a year now, the credit has been quite good. Recently, Wang Tengjiao, the manager of the Bureau, believed that the previously issued 500,000 yuan was only sufficient for circulation in the above-mentioned places, and planned to continue issuing 1 million yuan (600,000 yuan for two 角 notes and 400,000 yuan for one 角 notes) for distribution throughout the province. After submitting a request to the Department of Finance for review, Wang Xiangrong, the Director of the Department of Finance, immediately submitted it to the Provincial Government meeting for discussion. As a result, it was passed as it was. The document submitted to the Provincial Government is recorded on the left: (According to the report submitted by Wang Tengjiao, the manager of the Shandong Ping 市 Official Money Bureau, the Bureau's previous printing of 500,000 yuan of 角 Notes, the city needs about 200,000 yuan for circulation, Weixian, Jining, Tengxian, and Linqing need about 160,000 yuan in total, and Qingdao, Yantai, Longkou, Zhoucun, Boshan, and Tai'an need about 140,000 yuan in total. The printed 角 Notes are only sufficient for the application of the above-mentioned places, and it is proposed to continue printing 600,000 yuan of two 角 Notes and 400,000 yuan of one 角 Notes, totaling 1 million yuan, for distribution and application. The China East Printing Bureau, which printed the 角 Notes last time, is about to finish, and it is ordered to continue to undertake the work. The machinery is complete, and the workers are skilled. Not only can the printing cost be saved, but the completion date will be faster. If approved, the value will be negotiated with the Bureau again, and a contract will be signed. Please check and instruct, etc. Based on this, it is found that it is now the time to unify the currency system in the province and ban private paper money issuance. The 500,000 yuan of 角 Notes printed by the Bureau are not sufficient for use, and it is necessary to continue printing and issuing them. It is proposed to approve the printing of 1 million yuan of 角 Notes for circulation. It should be submitted for check and instruction, etc. Whether it should be approved or not, please make a public decision.)

▲ Robbery with Injury at Huchuan Bridge: At the home of Mao Shunming, a farmer in Xihe Township, Eighteenth Ward, Huchuan Bridge in the county, over twenty robbers speaking with a Henan accent suddenly arrived on the night before. Suzhou 92

▲ Epidemic Prevention Work on Donghou Mountain: The Dengshan Hospital, founded on this mountain, has been in operation for five years and has achieved remarkable results. Every summer, it increases the number of temporary epidemic hospitals. This summer, due to the aftermath of the Battle of Shanghai, epidemic outbreaks are inevitable. Hospital Director Yan Jingru, together with Western-trained doctor Shi Ruxin, have been administering preventative vaccines. Although there have been a few cases recently, they have been treated by the hospital and are safe. It is also reported that the hospital's expenses are fully covered by the board of directors and does not charge medical or pharmaceutical fees.

▲ Dispute over the Price of Foreign Small Change: The County Chamber of Commerce previously received instructions from the Ministry of Finance, based on a consultation from the Ministry of Industry. The Silk and Satin Guild of Jintan County stated that the Suzhou money changers were suppressing the price of small change, harming all industries, and requested that this be stopped. The County Chamber of Commerce was instructed to investigate and report back. According to the reply, the Suzhou price of small change fluctuates in accordance with Shanghai. Even if all industries are harmed by the small change price, it is the result of market conditions. The Suzhou money changers have no intention of deliberately suppressing the price. The County Chamber of Commerce submitted a report to the Ministry of Finance for review on the 9th.

▲ Water Police Launch Major Campaign to Suppress Lake Bandits: Since last month, a large group of lake bandits has been hiding in West Taihu Lake, acting wildly. The bandit leader is Geng Mazi. On the morning of the 9th, District Head Shen personally led troops and took the Zhizhong motorboat to the area east and west of Ceting to conduct a search and suppression operation. Shen Baoyi, the commander of the Suzhou-Songjiang water bandit suppression force, will also personally lead a team to assist in the suppression starting today.

▲ Young Woman Commits Suicide Due to Poverty: A village woman, Wu, from Wu Jiaqiao in the Second District (Jingyun City), was destitute and owned only two mu of ash fertilizer fields. Her husband died early, leaving behind a son named Arong, who worked as a mason. Over ten years ago, she remarried Zhou Apei from Zhouxiang Village in a neighboring village. When Apei entered the Wu family, he brought his own fields with him. Soon after, they had a son and a daughter. Four or five years ago, Apei arranged for Arong, the son from her previous marriage, to marry Hua, a woman from Zhangtang Bridge. Although they were not formally married, they lived together. However, the Wu family was not wealthy and had very limited funds. A month ago, Hua owed a piece of summer cloth and asked Arong for money to repay the debt. Arong promised to pay it after he received his wages from a certain household. However, his mother had taken the wages. A quarrel broke out between the mother and son. Hua, witnessing this, felt hopeless and thought the future was bleak. On the morning of the 7th, at 8:00 AM, she entered her room and hanged herself. When her family discovered her, it was too late. Afterwards, Hua's family rushed to the Wu family to negotiate, demanding that she be buried in an elaborate coffin. The Wu family only had two sheng of rice and two yuan left. They did not know how to cover the expenses. The body had not been placed in a coffin as of 4:00 PM on the 8th, which is truly tragic.

Special Article

On Summer Vacation Homework: Ya. 97

Summer vacation is the golden time for students. During this time, they can get closer to nature and expand the walls of the classroom to all aspects of society. They can not only learn from lively things but also try to do what they love in the real society. Unfortunately, during summer vacation in our country, due to excessive indulgence after separation from family and the disruption of a relatively structured life, there is an increase in the chances of illness and death.

The summer vacation of the 21st year is coming. This is the first summer vacation nearly ten months after the loss of the Northeast and nearly half a year after the Shanghai disaster. During this month, most male and female students will embark on their summer vacation journey home.

What to do during summer vacation? This is what every student should ask themselves before rolling up their bedding. I will introduce a few suggestions to everyone.

(1) Deeply Imprint the Scars of National Crisis on the People: You still have to skip classes to give speeches at school. Now is the best opportunity. Students above the middle school level can gather comrades to start summer schools or training classes in various villages to promote awareness of the national crisis and improve farmers' knowledge. (2) Investigate Enemy Goods in Detail: Thoroughly investigate the names, quantities, transportation methods, and main stores selling enemy goods in various places, and find ways to boycott them. (3) Travel to Various Places: Within the limits of economic possibility, everyone should travel to various places. This is lively education and very beneficial. (4) Try to Make Various Specimens: Such as local agricultural products and all kinds of animals and minerals. If specimens can be made and everyone brings them together after the summer, it will definitely help teaching.

(5) Get Close to Nature: The physical fitness of students in our country is generally not very healthy, and there are even more psychological health deficiencies. This is especially harmful to students in cities. This originally concerns economic, political, and social aspects, but being too isolated from nature is a major reason. Everyone should take advantage of the summer vacation to go to the countryside and the forest to awaken from confused dreams and sorrows and lead life to a more pleasant and easy path.

(6) Review or Preview Lessons: Make a general review of past lessons or try to preview future lessons. Everyone knows this is beneficial.

The above are just some of the larger points of summer vacation homework that everyone can do, but to achieve considerable results, the following two points are very important:

(1) Maintain a Relatively Structured Life: Irregular eating and sleeping habits not only hinder summer vacation homework but also greatly impair health, especially in the summer.

(2) There Must Be No Exceptions: Things that should be done at a certain time and things that should not be done must not be an exception for special reasons. If there are exceptions, everything is over.

Young students, do not let sleeping, gluttony, and indulgence attack you again during the 21st year summer vacation. I hope you happily accept the arrival of the summer vacation and make progressive use of the long summer vacation. To do this, you must first have a work plan.

National Conference of Presidents of Universities and Colleges Held Today 98

The conference of presidents of national universities and colleges, convened by the Ministry of Education, was originally scheduled to be held yesterday (the 10th), but was postponed to the 11th in the conference hall of the Ministry of Education because the presidents of the various schools had not yet arrived. The news of the conference is recorded below.

(1) Presidents Who Have Arrived in Beijing: As of the evening of the 10th, the following presidents had arrived: Cai Yuanpei, President of the Academia Sinica; Duan Xipeng, President of Central University; Jiang Menglin, President of Peking University; Wang Shijie, President of Wuhan University; Hu Shuhua, President of Tongji University; Yang Zhensheng, President of Qingdao University; Li Zhaohuan, President of Jiaotong University; Lin Fengmian, President of the Art Institute; Xiao Youmei, President of the Music Institute; Chu Minyi, President of the Sino-French University; Zheng Hongnian, President of Jinan University (represented by Chen Zhongfan); Cai Yuanze, President of Beiyang Institute of Technology (represented by Wang Jixu). The following presidents had not yet arrived in Beijing: Li Shizeng, President of the Peiping Research Institute; Zou Lu, President of Zhongshan University; Shen Yinmo, President of Peiping University; Li Zheng, President of Peiping Normal University; Mei Yiqi, President of Tsinghua University; Cheng Tianfang, President of Zhejiang University; Wang Zhaorong, President of Sichuan University (the Ministry of Communications will not attend); Xie Yingzhou, President of Guangzhou Law School. Except for Zou Lu, Xie Yingzhou, and Li Shizeng, the remaining presidents are on their way and should be able to arrive in time to attend. Guo Xinsong, Director of Higher Education of the Ministry of Education, has returned to his hometown and the Ministry of Education sent a telegram yesterday urging him to return quickly to participate in the conference.

(2) Nature of the Conference: This conference has no resolution form. The Ministry of Education, in accordance with the Chen Guofu education reform plan decided by the central government, will solicit the opinions of the presidents on the point that each university should increase the number of colleges of agriculture, engineering, medicine, and science, as a reference for reforming higher education. In addition, the issue of funding for each university is also the focus of this conference.

(3) Proposals from the Ministry of Education: It is heard that the Ministry of Education has prepared the following outlines of proposals, and the reasons will be explained orally. They will be submitted at the meeting. Proposal outlines: 1. Proposal to increase the number of colleges of agriculture, engineering, medicine, and science. 2. Proposal that national universities located in the same region should avoid duplication of departments. 3. Proposal that each university should cultivate talents for national defense construction. 4. Proposal for university funding. 5. Proposal to limit the teaching of professors. 6. Proposal for university graduation exams. 7. Proposal for improving military training. 8. Proposal on how to rectify the academic atmosphere of the school. 9. Proposal on the employment of graduates.

(4) Proposals from Xiao and Lin: Xiao Youmei, President of the National Music Institute, proposed two proposals: (1) (The National Music Institute requests the prompt issuance of temporary funds to purchase a school site and construct school buildings). (2) (The National Music Institute proposes to restore the college system and name) (Seconded by Lin Fengmian). Lin Fengmian, President of the National Hangzhou Art Institute, proposed to the conference (proposes to add a college of art to Article 6 of the University Organization Law to improve art education and restore the college organization).

Jiangsu Education Department Designates 101

Seven Middle Schools and Experimental Elementary Schools to be Converted into Affiliated Elementary Schools

▲ And Reassigns Those in Charge of the Affiliated Elementary Schools

The Jiangsu Education Department previously designated eight provincial middle schools. Starting from the 21st year, they will focus on running normal schools. The experimental elementary schools of the designated seven middle schools will be converted into affiliated elementary schools. As Gaozhong Middle School originally did not have an experimental elementary school, an affiliated elementary school will now be added, totaling eight affiliated elementary schools. Each school will have one person in charge. Several regulations regarding affiliated elementary schools have been issued. The names of those reassigned to be in charge of each affiliated elementary school are listed below: Zhenzhong Middle School: Shen Shanzhi (original principal of the experimental elementary school, Xie Jizeng, reassigned); Xizhong Middle School: Pan Ren (original principal of the experimental elementary school, Zhu Yanhe, resigned); Ruzhong Middle School: Zhang Wenheng (newly established); Taizhong Middle School: Gong Jiaqin (original principal of the experimental elementary school); Huaiyin Middle School: Xu Tao (original principal of the experimental elementary school); Donghaizhong Middle School: Yang Naijin (original principal of the experimental elementary school); Su Girls Middle School: Chen Dingxiu (original principal of the experimental elementary school); Xu Girls Middle School: Chen Suyu (original principal of the experimental elementary school). In addition, the principals of the provincial experimental elementary schools will not be changed, except for Zhang Zhongyuan, who will be reassigned to the experimental elementary school of Nantong Middle School. Jin Yingyuan (Yangzhong Experimental Elementary School) and Shen Zishan (Nan Girls Middle School Experimental Elementary School) will be changed to full-time positions.

Death of Female Educator Zhu Xuejing 104

Shanghai female educator Zhu Xuejing, style name Danru, daughter of Zhu Kongwen, a local jurist, and wife of Zhang Zhonghuan, secretary of the Provincial Shanghai Middle School, after graduating from Beijing Women's Higher Normal School, successively served as a Chinese language teacher at Xiamen Jimei Normal School, director of discipline and Chinese language teacher at the Provincial Women's Sericulture School, and Chinese language teacher at Jingye Middle School. She was currently serving as a Chinese language teacher at the Provincial Shanghai Middle School. She was passionate about education, excelled in Chinese studies, and was a talented figure in the Jiangsu female education circles, highly respected by teachers and friends. Unfortunately, she passed away at midnight on the 10th of this month due to postpartum complications. Friends and relatives were grieved to hear the news. The funeral is scheduled for 3:00 PM on the 11th at the Wanguo Funeral Parlor on Jiaozhou Road. It is certain that a wave of mourning will occur with a plain carriage and a white horse.

Exhibition of Relics from the War Zone Has Opened 105

▲ Open Daily from 1:00 PM to 7:00 PM

The exhibition of relics from the Shanghai war zone features works by the famous painter Wang Jiyuan, who personally went to the war zone to realistically depict the relics. It opened on the 9th and will run until the 14th at the Jiyuan Xunqin Painting Studio at No. 90 Route Lubaud, corner of Avenue Massenet. It is heard that after the opening, watercolor paintings such as No. 5 (A Scorched Earth), No. 9 (Shenzaobang), No. 11 (Labor University's Bell Tower), No. 16 (Jiangwan After the Catastrophe), and No. 18 (Wusong, Ashes After the Looting) have been reserved for collection by guests. All the works are heartbreaking to see and are full of the tragic conditions and remnants of the war of resistance. At a time when the movement to end the civil war is being promoted, witnessing this will be even more alarming.

The Establishment of Kaiming Middle School 106

Educational circles in this city, including Sun Jiwu and others, recognizing the importance of secondary education, have jointly established the private Kaiming Middle School. The school is located next to the Xie Bridge Xietu Road Manufacturing Bureau Road Bethel Hospital (formerly the site of Huiling Middle School). The school building is a Western-style three-story building with more than sixty rooms, as well as a spacious campus and sports field, capable of accommodating more than 400 students. The establishment has been approved by the Municipal Education Bureau. It is reported that the Chairman of the School Board is Shen Yizhen, the Principal is Cheng Keyou, and the remaining faculty and staff are being hired successively. They have served in the education field for many years and have a well-established reputation. It is also reported that the school has determined the implementation plan, the curriculum strives for practicality and vocational training, the junior high school does not separate departments, the senior high school separates general and commercial departments, and implements strict training based on the principle of unity of education and training. The school will soon publish the enrollment examination date, set for July 24.

Public Tennis Doubles Final 107

Zheng Yu Wins Championship

▲ Defeats the two Guos in straight sets

The Shanghai Chinese Tennis Club's open doubles championship concluded yesterday. Young players Zheng Zhaojia and Yu Tianguang defeated Guo Qida and Guo Pengnian 7-5, 6-0, 6-3 in the final. The championship was won by Zheng and Yu. After the game, the silver cup was awarded by tennis veteran Hu Yun. The referee was Lin Baohua.

▲ The two Guos seize the initiative. The competition began at four o'clock under the gaze of a few spectators at the Chinese tennis court. The two Guos won two games in a row, showing a strong momentum to seize the initiative. Then, with a 5-3 lead, they had a superior situation. However, Zheng and Yu did not be discouraged, and calmly advanced, winning four games in a row, reversing the situation to win 7-5.

▲ Zheng and Yu take the prize easily. In the second set, the two Guos were at a loss. Zheng and Yu completed six games in one go, ending the set. In the third set, the two Guos failed 3-6 despite Zheng and Yu's mediocre playing style.

▲ Zheng and Yu excel at net play. Among the four players, Zheng Zhaojia performed the best. His forehand and backhand shots are sharp and extraordinary. And Zheng and Yu's net play is quite skilled, which is a major problem for their opponents. Guo Qida is known for his calmness, but he is not good at dealing with fast balls, and Guo's slow balls just suit Zheng and Yu's tastes, giving them a chance to create a masterful performance. Guo Pengnian's performance was mediocre, making Guo feel that he was unable to support the game alone.

Finance 116

The price of silver bullion fluctuated greatly last week.

New highs appeared for three days at the beginning of the week.

Selling pressure was strong at the end of the week, and the price plummeted.

The price of silver bullion fluctuated drastically last week, with turbulent waves and daily fluctuations of more than ten taels. The situation was confusing and unstoppable. It opened at a surge of 10 taels and 1 qian at the beginning of the week, breaking through 760 taels, a total of 63 and a half taels. This was because the silver market had shrunk due to bank closures after the settlement and holidays. Subsequently, the local foreign exchange market also tightened, and large short positions rushed to cover, so the price frequently rose sharply, advancing straight ahead without looking back, rising sharply for more than 20 taels in three days, and suddenly reaching a new high of 780 taels and 8 qian. On Thursday, the rising trend began to subside, and the price fluctuated slightly around 770 taels. However, it was heard that the Lausanne Conference would have a signed resolution, people's hearts turned downward, and the market turned from strong to weak. Selling pressure surged, causing a sharp drop of more than 20 taels. At the weekend, it suddenly broke through 760 taels, totaling 58 taels. There were also reports that Lausanne had signed an agreement. The final closing price was 61 taels and 4 qian. In these six days, there was a retracement of 22 taels and 8 qian, and the overall comparison was still up 8 taels before the closure (June 30) (already up for five consecutive weeks, about 40 taels). As for the London and New York silver markets, there was a slight rebound. The local foreign exchange market was quoted at a par for shillings and a continued reduction of 25 cents for US dollars, but there was no glory or disgrace within the banks. The exchange rate has rebounded after falling for four consecutive weeks. It is estimated that the exchange rate is one point for British against US, and 9375 for US against British. The daily transaction volume of British and American exchange rates in the gold industry is quite prosperous, but there are many differences in arbitrage, and most of them are hedging. The settlement price is 67 taels, with a daily difference of 10 taels. The spot bare price was initially increased by about 10 taels, and later saw a low of 7 taels and 7 qian 5 fen. Each number's August chips are estimated to be about 20,000 pieces. Daily trading is more agile than in the previous two weeks, but the two sides of the long and short sides sometimes have a double-sided control trend. The financial industry during this hot summer season is usually a dull period. This time, the government's use of the foreign silver standard has attracted special attention, and various market conditions have mostly erupted, especially the price of foreign silver is the most important, and the increase is also the most significant. Yesterday was Sunday, and banks were not trading as usual, but the competition for the price of silver in the market continued to rise. The early market was 6 qian 9 fen 4 li half, which seemed to be 1 li and a half higher than the early market the day before. The afternoon market was slightly softer at 125, at 6 qian 9 fen 4 li 3 hao 7 and a half, resulting in an increase of 1 li 375. Securities: The Bond Market Was Very Quiet Last Week 118

▲ Prices were also extremely sluggish, with mutual ups and downs compared to the previous period

The market situation of the local Chinese Securities Exchange during the past week (from July 4 to 9) was that, after just settling accounts, business needed to be reorganized, and the situation and diplomatic situation had not improved. The popularity of major investors showed no signs of recovery, and even sporadic transactions were not many. Therefore, the market was very clear. The spot market only traded 149,500 yuan in the whole week, including 25,000 yuan of 96 public bonds, 1,000 yuan of 20 customs, 17,000 yuan of customs duties, 13,000 yuan of consolidated tax, 12,000 yuan of 20 volumes, 10,000 yuan of 19 customs, and 78,000 yuan each. Futures were 2.34 million on Monday, Tuesday, and Friday, and 1.67 million yuan on other days, totaling 12.455 million yuan. The clarity of the market was rare, as the turnover in the past was more than double that of this time. The internal salt tax was 2.68 million yuan, the consolidated tax was 2.27 million yuan, the 20 customs was 1.825 million yuan, the 20 volumes was 1.475 million yuan, the 19 good was 1.125 million yuan, the disarmament was 1.165 million yuan, the 19 customs was 850,000 yuan, the disbandment was 655,000 yuan, the customs duty was 180,000 yuan, the organization was 600,000 yuan, the six-percent organization was 195,000 yuan, and the 96 public bonds were 35,000 yuan. Although the August futures have been open for many days, the entry and exit are extremely rare, with a total of only more than 300,000 yuan for various bonds. As for the changes in the prices of various bonds during the past week, the ring was dull, the demand was very flat, and the price was always in a state of rotation, resulting in the fact that the exchange's futures reserves were not large, and investors were unwilling to make large-scale sales at this time, while the sellers were also very flat due to the market and had concerns, and did not dare to sell short at low prices. The financial industry, even more, was unwilling to sell off and suppress the market price. This is why the market has always been very flat, and the bond prices are often trapped in sluggishness and difficult to have large fluctuations. After observing the changes in the past week, the market trended upward on Monday, and fell back on Tuesday and Wednesday. After that, there were mutual ups and downs. As a result, compared with the previous week, except for a few August futures that rose more sharply, the remaining mutual ups and downs were only about half a yuan. Cotton Yarn 119

The yarn market fluctuated greatly last week.

Started rising and then falling... spot demand is strong.

The cotton yarn market was very fierce at the beginning of last week, and people's hearts were fluctuating. Due to the poor climate of American cotton and serious pest news, raw cotton rose sharply, driving the yarn market. Both the long and short sides had considerable strength, so the market fluctuated more and more, suddenly high and suddenly low, making people fall into a fog. At the same time, the Yunnan and Guangdong gangs in the southern port searched for spot yarn in the market, and the July and August goods of some yarn factories were all absorbed. On Tuesday, American cotton suddenly rose 30 points, breaking through the 6-point mark. It was said that the Lausanne Conference had signed an agreement, and foreign prices might rise. Therefore, people's hearts were unusually sharp, and Rongxing's long side bought more when it fell. On Wednesday, the market trended tighter and the popularity was strong. The highest price of the October standard yarn was 147 taels. At the weekend, although the US cotton government's acreage report decreased, the market price rose slightly. Generally, large investors tended to sell short, and it was said that Japanese merchants were destroying everywhere in the rear. As a result, the selling trend suddenly became strong, and the market price turned down sharply. In short, the current situation has not yet entered a stable path, and there are still ups and downs. The customer gang bought a total of 23,281 packages of various yarns this week. The Yunnan, Guangdong, and Fujian gangs bought the most, and the other gangs rarely moved. The standard yarn was quite strong at the beginning of the week, but tended to be tired at the weekend. The result of each month was 23 qian higher than the price of the previous week. The total transaction volume of the whole week was 229,300 packages. The amount purchased by each gang is recorded separately below.

Standard Cotton Was Firm Last Week 120

The cotton market was very sharp at the beginning of the week, with more buyers and fewer sellers, and the market was firm. The reason was that the report of American cotton pest was serious, and the situation tended to rise, which made people in this city optimistic, and generally major investors towed in to do more, so the market had a continuous rise and increase trend. On Tuesday, the American cotton telegraph came and rose 30 points, and the gold price also rose 20 taels. The hard atmosphere in the market was extremely fierce. The highest price of standard cotton was 32 taels and 7 qian. At that time, it was said that Japanese merchants bought 230,000 dan in the market, so the popularity became tighter and tighter, and some turned from short to long. At the weekend, although the government's acreage estimates were released less, the weather turned sunny, people's hearts turned tired, and the market suddenly fell by 89 qian. As a result, the price of standard cotton in each month rose by 23 qian compared to the previous week. There was still no import volume of spot cotton from this factory. It is said that Japanese merchants bought a huge amount. The transaction volume of standard cotton in one week was 593,400 dan. The source on the wharf was 2,490 packages of Yaohua cotton. American cotton fell 5 points compared to the previous week. The situation of the cotton market still needs to be shifted by American cotton. Grain Prices: Rice Market Weak and Sluggish 122

▲South Shanghai: Yesterday, approximately twenty ships arrived from various routes. There was a slight increase in warehouse stock. Sales in urban and rural shops remained sluggish. The Zhabei market was weak, and there was a large inventory. Sentiment was bearish. The price of both thick and thin japonica rice dropped slightly. Although the price of premium *lu yang* rice was sporadically affected by imported rice, the market became increasingly weak. Sales of low-quality *bian yuan* rice were thin and slow, and the market was generally stable.

▲Zhabei: Yesterday's rice market saw few deliveries from the west, and river inventories were still high. In terms of local transactions, due to the clear weather, buyers were hesitant. Regular and standard japonica rice, as well as Zhongguan rice, fell by one or two *jiao*. Premium imported rice was scarce, and the market appeared quite ordinary. Arrivals of *bian yin yuan* rice were weak, and sales were relatively good, keeping the market firm. Imported rice warehouses were very full, and customer demand was stagnant. Local sales were also thin, causing prices to continue to decline.

Sugar Market 123

Raw Sugar Initially Fell, Then Recovered

▲Icing Sugar Very Popular at Opening

Yesterday, the Sugar Market Association's trading was quite active. However, buying interest was relatively calm, and offered prices were slightly lower. Sellers were willing to compromise, which slightly lowered market prices. Dutch sugar number 24 raw white was traded at 14 *liang* 4 *qian* 2.5 *fen*. The market was steady. Local icing sugar was offered at 12 *liang*, and then 300-400 bags were traded at 11 *liang* 9.5 *qian*, making it very popular. Number 8 Dutch red sugar from Huaxin opened at 10 *liang* 6 *qian*, with an offering of 1,500 bags. Buyers were very interested, but their bid was 10 *liang* 5 *qian*. Negotiations were ongoing and no transaction had been completed.

Dried Goods: First Batch of Jinshan Mushrooms Arrives 124

A certain firm in the South Shanghai market rushed to transport over ten boxes of new Jinshan mushrooms the day before yesterday. Yesterday, they appeared on the market for the first time. The quality was not particularly high, but the quantity was small. Therefore, whole mushrooms were priced at 25 *liang* and flattened mushrooms at 32 *liang* 6 *qian*. If high-quality goods arrive in later batches, market prices will fluctuate.

Textiles: Woolen Fabrics Market Sales Sluggish 125

Sales of woolen fabrics have been extremely sluggish recently. The hot weather has stifled actual demand. There are only sporadic sales in the local market, and buying interest from merchant guilds has gradually decreased. Because of a surge of fifty *liang* in remittance rates, the Sichuan merchant guild stopped making purchases. Overall, the atmosphere in the trade association was scattered. Both explicit and implicit prices were soft. Currently, Yongfeng 8686 *fanghua deng su bi ji* is selling for 2 *liang* 3 *qian* 2.5 *fen*, Ningfeng Pengshoutu is 3 *liang* 4.5 *qian*, and Gongping Sizi Gaosheng is 2 *liang* 4 *qian* 2.5 *fen*.

Local News

Disturbance at the North Railway Station Yesterday 126

▲Over One Hundred Communists Demonstrating to Demand Reduced Prices

▲Shouting Slogans Explaining Noulens

▲More Than Twenty Apprehended

Yesterday morning around 11:30, over one hundred communists converged at the North Railway Station, planning a demonstration. As a large group of communists was entering the station, two workers, Wen Kaifu from Qingjiang and Shen Asan from Hubei, both around thirty years old, were searched by Fifth District police officers stationed at the station entrance. They were found to be carrying communist leaflets demanding the release of the Noulens and threatening riots and bloodshed. They were immediately taken to the Fifth District Headquarters for questioning. It was learned that a large number of communists had already infiltrated the North Railway Station. As a precaution, the Fifth District authorities dispatched a large number of armed police officers to patrol the area around the station. Upon hearing the news, the Concession police immediately sent a large number of detectives in an armored car, parked at the intersection of Boundary Road and Kennaugh Road. The detectives patrolled the area from the intersection of Boundary Road and靶子 Road to North Zhejiang Road. Seeing the increased security, the communists gradually dispersed around 12:30. About forty communists remained inside the station. At 12:45, a Changshu-Shanghai passenger train arrived at the station. These forty communists mingled with the passengers, distributing communist leaflets, and shouting slogans such as "Down with imperialism!", "Oppose the arrest of the Noulens!", "Support the Soviet Red Army!", and "Release communist political prisoners!" They continued shouting as they exited the station. As they reached Boundary Road, Concession detectives arrested more than twenty. The rest managed to escape. To prevent a riot, the Zhabei military and police authorities dispatched the Second Battalion, led by Captain Liu Wanjun of the 8th Company of the Republican Road Security Force, with over one hundred security guards, to the area in front of the North Railway Station, from Baoshan Road to the Han Bridge, to maintain order at 3:00 in the afternoon.

The Hebei Fellow Villagers Association sent a telegram to various organizations in Hebei Province (titles omitted): We have read the news from Nanjing in the Shanghai newspaper dated the fourth. Looking back, the loss of the Northeast has been over half a year in an instant, only because calls for help were unheeded. This has left thirty million people under the oppressive rule. Patriotic individuals who occasionally rise up are immediately killed. People are living cautiously and tolerating humiliation to survive. However, the avarice of the invaders has not ended and they are plotting to invade Tianjin and Peking. They want to enthrone a puppet emperor and take control of China. We, the fellow villagers from Hebei in Shanghai, witness the imminent loss of our homeland. We are saddened by the ignorance of officials and the death of patriotism. While the national crisis continues, shoddy goods flood the market. While the Northeast has not been recovered, the people act as if they have nothing to worry about. Do not think that because we have vast lands and a large population, we are safe. Be aware that in modern times, it is easy to destroy a country using scientific methods. The neighboring power is focused on aggression, while our court is solely concerned with power and position.
