We resist external powers' aggression and boycott shoddy goods, cutting off the Japanese market in North China. If we are determined, there is a way to save ourselves. Observe the Battle of Shanghai, where the people of Southeast China enthusiastically resisted the enemy. With a single army, they resisted over a hundred thousand enemy troops for forty days. This proves that with unity and sacrifice, we can survive. If we remain unenlightened and miss this opportunity, then the cries of the people of the Northeast will remain in our ears. What more can the people of Annam, India, and Korea say? We present these anxious words with utmost urgency.

Japanese 129

Monopolize Northeast Finance

▲Li Fangxin Discusses After Returning From the Eastern Provinces

The finance of Northeast China has been in a state of chaos since the September 18 Incident. Recently, the Japanese have again used the puppet state to organize a central bank, which has resulted in the replacement of the previously existing local banks. These new banks have also issued paper money and silver coins to replace the currently circulating national currency. A reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency interviewed Li Fang, the former manager of the Bank of Communications in the three eastern provinces, who had just returned from the eastern provinces, to discuss the situation in detail. The following is a summary of the interview.

▲Japanese Currency Monopolizes the Eastern Provinces: The finance of the Three Eastern Provinces has been monopolized by the Japanese. In terms of the current currency system, the amount of Japanese gold coins in circulation is approximately 3 million yuan, and the amount of gold notes is approximately 130 million yuan. Forty percent of these gold notes circulate within Korea, and the remainder circulates in South Manchuria. Since the September 18th Incident, the amount of gold notes has increased by at least 10 to 20 million yuan, so the amount of gold notes circulating in the Eastern Provinces should be over 100 million yuan, worth approximately 150 million yuan in national currency. The amount of our national currency in circulation is approximately 60 million yuan in foreign currency issued by the six banks in Harbin, worth approximately 45 to 60 million yuan. The current silver dollars issued by the Fengtian Four Banks Reserve were approximately 4 to 5 million yuan after the Liaoning Incident, worth only 2 to 3 million yuan. The silver dollar notes issued by the Yongheng Official Bank in Jilin are worth approximately 7 million yuan. The silver dollar notes issued by the Heilongjiang Official Bank are worth approximately 12 to 13 million yuan. The exchange notes from various banks in Tianjin that have flowed into the Eastern Provinces are worth only 4 to 5 million yuan, for a total of 80 to 90 million yuan, which is about half the amount of Japanese currency and is entirely controlled by the Japanese.

▲Puppet Currency Usurps National Currency: After the September 18th Incident, the Japanese army seized control of financial institutions wherever they went. They have now established a puppet bank and announced unified currency measures. The currency unit is silver, with a purity of 23.91 grams of silver. The standard set by our country's currency regulations is 4 *fen* 8 *li* of Kuping pure silver, equivalent to 24.17 grams, which is a difference of eleven parts per thousand. Their intention is to prevent our country's currency from circulating in the Eastern Provinces. Because the people of the Eastern Provinces see that the silver color of our country's currency is better than that of the puppet state's currency, they use it at the same price, which is not cost-effective. Therefore, they will collect it or melt it down in batches to recast it, so that in the future, no coins made by our country will be seen in the Northeast.

▲Elimination of Financial Institutions: For the old currency of the Eastern Provinces, the Japanese have stipulated that except for the currency issued by the Bank of Communications and the Bank of China, which may be used temporarily for five years, all other currencies must be withdrawn within two years and replaced with paper currency from the puppet central bank. The existing local banks, that is, the official banks in various places, have now been changed to branches of the puppet central bank, and will be completely and thoroughly changed within two years. In other words, they will be eliminated and reorganized by the Japanese. All old currency from official banks will only be maintained until the end of this year and will be cleared separately before being merged into the puppet central bank when the time comes.

▲New Paper Currency to Be Issued: After the establishment of the puppet central bank, it will be supervised and managed by the Japanese, and a policy of using paper currency to absorb cash will be implemented. A large number of banknotes will be issued and are currently being printed. They will soon be circulating in the puppet state. The Japanese are also preparing to mint silver coins, and they plan to repair the mint near the Shenyang Arsenal and then begin production.

▲Chinese Society Gives Public Lecture: The Chinese Economic Research Association invited Li Fang to give a lecture at the Chinese Society on Zanghaiwei Road yesterday on the financial situation in the Northeast. Many people attended the lecture.

Lin Wojiang Discusses 130

Plans to Expand Air Defense

▲Improve Facilities and Training at Aviation Schools

▲Huang Bingheng Comes to Shanghai to Connect with Various Sectors

The Aviation Department recently launched a major plan to expand air defense. Lin Wojiang, legal commissioner of the department, arrived in Shanghai yesterday. A reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency visited him and received a detailed account of the expansion plan, which is summarized below.

▲Improve Aviation Schools: The Aviation Department's aviation school was initially established in Nanjing and has now been moved to Hangzhou. Its monthly budget is set at 500,000 yuan. The equipment and technical training are very rudimentary, hence the discussion to expand it. The Aviation Department plans to increase the monthly budget, expand enrollment, and hire more instructors. Recently, the National Government hired Colonel Jouett, an American aviation expert, and eleven others to go to Hangzhou to plan the expansion of the aviation school.

▲Increase Aircraft Purchases: The most elite of our country's aviation aircraft, the Northeast Flying Corps of over two hundred aircraft, were all seized by the Japanese after the September 18th Incident. The existing Central Flying Corps is not sufficient for national defense, so they plan to purchase aircraft from overseas in the shortest possible time and will implement this plan when the funding is available.

▲Huang Comes to Shanghai: The Air Defense National Salvation Association, organized by various sectors, is taking shape. Huang Bingheng, the director of the Aviation Department, came to Shanghai last night to discuss aviation matters with the association and plans to host a banquet today for Wang Xiaolai, Li Fusun, Wang Zhengting, and others to request their assistance with air defense matters.

The Commercial Press 131

Held Shareholders' Meeting Yesterday

▲General Distribution Office Set to Reopen August 1

The Commercial Press held its annual shareholders' meeting for the 20th year yesterday afternoon at the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce. Present were 1,297 shareholders and representatives, holding 35,873 shares, representing 31,563 voting rights. The meeting began at 3:30 PM. Ding Feizhang was elected as chairman. The board of directors first reported on the destruction of the company and the handling of the aftermath. This included: the amount of losses, retained personnel, emergency relocation, handling of debts, collection of customer accounts, maintaining branch offices, preparing for the autumn book sales, providing relief to employees, dismissing some employees, clearing the general factory's post-disaster expenses, and preparing for reopening. Next, they reported on the company's operating status for the 20th year, stating that the total operations of the company were much better than the previous year and that the company had experienced more growth this year than in recent years. Unexpectedly, just as the closing of accounts began, the national disaster struck, causing significant losses and turning profits into losses, with a total loss of 3,471,283 yuan. They then reported the company's asset inventory. Afterwards, supervisor Zhou Xinbo reported on the inspection of the accounts. After the reports were completed, the board of directors' reports were adopted. Then, a motion was proposed to use the general reserve to offset the losses, stating that the total loss was over 3.47 million yuan and that the existing general reserve of over 1.33 million yuan would be used to offset the losses, resulting in a net loss of over 2.13 million yuan. This motion was passed. Subsequently, a proposal was made to reduce capital to 2.5 million yuan and amend the company's articles of association. After discussion, the chairman announced that because the reduction of capital and amendment of the articles of association were significant matters, it was decided that each shareholder would take the proposals back for careful study and that the board of directors would schedule a special shareholders' meeting to discuss them again. The election of directors and supervisors then took place. The elected directors were Xia Xiaofang, Gao Hanqing, Bao Qinglin, Zhang Jusheng, Wang Yunwu, Li Bake, Zhang Chanfen, Ding Feizhang, Gao Mengdan, Liu Zhanen, Ye Kuichu, Guo Bingwen, and Huang Hanliang, thirteen in total. Subsequently, Bao Qingjia, Wang Kangsheng, and Zhang Tinggui were elected with a majority. The elected supervisors were Xu Fengshi, Xu Jiquing, and Zhou Xinbo, three in total. Subsequently, Zhao Fuzhuo and Xu Yizhuang were elected with a majority. The meeting adjourned around 7:00 PM. It was also reported that the company's Shanghai General Distribution Office is scheduled to reopen on August 1.

Job Losses in the 132

Chinese Pharmaceutical Industry

Employees' Meeting Prevented

▲Pharmaceutical Workers' Union to Hold Emergency Meeting Today

▲Representatives from Hangzhou Returned Yesterday After Mediation

The labor dispute in the local Chinese pharmaceutical industry remains unresolved. The union has scheduled an emergency meeting for 1:00 PM today to discuss the direction forward. Yesterday's unemployment meeting was prevented by the authorities. Details are as follows:

▲Unemployment Meeting Prevented: The delegation of unemployed workers in the pharmaceutical industry planned to hold a general assembly of all unemployed workers at the Yaowang Temple yesterday at 9:00 AM to demand that various employers find jobs for the unemployed. The First Section of the Third Precinct of the Municipal Public Security Bureau sent police to prevent the meeting on the grounds that it had not been approved by party and government authorities in advance. The Pharmaceutical Workers' Union also attempted to persuade the workers to postpone the meeting, arguing that the general assembly of unemployed workers had not been approved by the full board of directors and supervisors. The unemployed members who attended the meeting appointed Yu Guiqing, Dong Kuizhang, Zhuang Yongfa, and three others to meet with Section Chief Jin Dianyuan, while also holding a meeting and electing Li Baokang, Chen Weiming, and Feng Shilin as chairmen of the presidium. They demanded that the union provide food and organize a fundraising team to petition the trade association within a certain timeframe. After being persuaded, they ended the meeting.

▲Representatives from Hangzhou Returned: A reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency yesterday interviewed representatives Ye Zifang and Wang Yongjian from the Hangzhou Pharmaceutical Workers' Union at Zhenhua Hotel, Room 49. They said that, during this time of national crisis and internal unrest, they had repeatedly seen reports of increasingly large labor disputes in Shanghai, which was not a blessing for society. Recently, they also noticed that labor disputes had arisen in the pharmaceutical industry. Although it was only a dispute with one firm, Feng Cunren, the situation appeared to be escalating. Due to industry connections, their union decided to send them to Shanghai at their own expense, partly to comfort their fellow union members and partly to investigate the cause of the dispute, hoping to find an opportunity to mediate and achieve a peaceful resolution as a third party. They had heard that the Feng Cunren store owner had indicated a willingness to make concessions, such as paying each worker 50 yuan and providing compensation for strike losses. The mediators were willing to find a way to mediate, and the issue of replacement workers, as a whole, could be discussed by a joint committee. However, seeing that mediation was unlikely to be effective, they withdrew from the role of third party and sent letters to the union and trade association to bid farewell. They added that, in this era of social poverty and economic bankruptcy, strikes were not a blessing for society, so they did not want to rush to judgment and would only watch for the union's victory, which would also bring them joy. They were filled with emotion. It was reported that the representatives had left Shanghai and returned to Hangzhou last night.

Electricity Workers' Union Expresses Concerns 133

The Dagong News Agency reported that the Shanghai Electric Power Company previously fired a large number of workers, which aroused the resentment of all workers. Recently, it has continued to fire Ma Jinsheng and seven others, which has made the situation even more serious. The union sent a letter of warning to the company yesterday and issued an emergency declaration. Details are as follows:

▲Emergency Declaration: The Shanghai Electric Power Company Workers' Union issued an emergency declaration yesterday, stating: "Fellow citizens, the harsh, cruel, and vicious treatment of our fellow workers by the Shanghai Electric Power Company has recently become indescribable. We have endured enough pain and can no longer tolerate it. Therefore, we must inform our fellow citizens of the true situation of the company's oppression and ask for your sympathy and assistance. Since the Shanghai Electric Power Company was sold by the Municipal Council to the current company, its oppressive and cruel treatment of workers has begun. First, it stripped us of all the rights we had under the agreement. Then, citing excuses such as business decline and reduced work, it fired a large number of our old and new factory workers. Although the union has repeatedly sent representatives to request reinstatement, the company has shown no sympathy and firmly refused. Even after party and government authorities sent representatives to negotiate, there was no significant effect. The unemployed workers are now suffering and have no one to turn to. All workers are deeply resentful. Recently, the company authorities continued to fire old workers such as Ma Jinsheng and seven others without reason. We cannot tolerate this constant and escalating attack on us. We are determined to fight the imperialist company with an indomitable spirit. If the employers continue to be unrepentant, then in order to protect our own interests and ensure the survival of all our fellow workers, we will take the most effective final action to deal with them. We hope that all our fellow citizens will give us guidance and practical assistance. We issue this declaration."

▲Letter of Warning: The Electric Power Company Workers' Union sent a letter of warning to the company yesterday regarding the unwarranted firing of workers, requesting a response within a specific timeframe. The original letter is as follows: "Dear Sir/Madam, this is to inform you that our members Ma Jinshan, Zhou Yunfu, Xu Genlin, and others have reported that your company fired them without reason on the 7th and 8th of this month. We were shocked to learn of this. When your company handled the takeover from the Municipal Council, it agreed that the rights of the original employees would remain valid and that employees could not be fired without reason. However, according to recent events, in addition to the 121 employees who have already been fired, which remains unresolved, you have fired seven more employees without reason. Our union workers are deeply resentful. After discussion by the union's full representative meeting, we demand that your company immediately reinstate Ma Jinshan and the other seven. Otherwise, we will not be responsible for any unexpected problems that may arise. Furthermore, if your company believes it has grounds for dismissal, it must inform us of the reasons within three days of receiving this letter. If our investigation finds that there were indeed mistakes, there will naturally be no problem. However, the 5% annual salary for pension must still be paid, and severance pay of six months must also be issued. We hope that your company will consider the workers' difficulties and resolve this dispute quickly and satisfactorily. This is of utmost importance. To the Shanghai Electric Power Company."

After the labor dispute in the local silk factory industry was resolved, all silk factories reopened yesterday morning. The Municipal Public Security Bureau sent police to protect the reopening. However, few workers returned to work in the Hongkou District. Details are as follows:

▲Zhabei District: Fifteen silk factories in the Zhabei District, including Fengtai Shenji, Ruifeng Yuji, and Jiufeng Dingji, reopened at once yesterday morning in accordance with the trade association's notification. The Sixth District Silk Reeling Workers' Union sent council members Yuan Yunlong, Yang Gengdi, Wu Suzhen, Yan Aizhu, and others to lead all the staff to each factory gate to persuade workers to return to work. The Fourth Precinct of the Municipal Public Security Bureau sent armed police officers to protect the reopening. By 6:00 AM, all the workers in the factories had returned to work.

▲Hongkou District: Ten silk factories in the Hongkou District, including Yichang Hou Furenji and Tongwei, reopened yesterday morning. The Fourth District Silk Reeling Workers' Union sent council members Zhu Xizhang, Le Xiaorong, and Chen Xiufu to each factory to persuade workers to return to work. The Third Section of the Fifth Precinct of the Municipal Public Security Bureau sent police to protect the reopening. By 10:00 AM, only 20% of the workers at the Tongwei and Yujing factories had returned to work. At the remaining eight factories, including Yichang, Yuncheng, Chancheng, Renji, and Xinlun, 70-80% of the workers had returned to work. The union sent representatives again in the afternoon to persuade the workers, and it is expected that all workers will have returned to work by today.

French Electric Company Labor Strike Yesterday Report 135

▲Today the Municipal Government Continues Negotiations with the French Consulate

▲The Labor Union Presents Twelve Demands

After the strike of all employees in the machinery department of the French-owned Water and Electricity Company, the municipal government and the French Consulate are negotiating a solution. The labor union has presented demands, and citizens have already been affected by the strike. The details are as follows:

▲Sunday Rest Situation　Yesterday was the fourth day of the strike. The strike committee decided, based on the resolution of the third strike committee meeting, to rest on Sunday. A special announcement was issued yesterday morning, stating: "Regarding the announcement, it has been resolved by the strike committee that July 10th (Sunday) will be a day of rest. All members are to comply. This is announced. However, members of the strike committee will still report to the office as usual. The picket line will continue to be on duty, with slightly relaxed vigilance. The iron gates of the company on Rue Lupan (Lu Ban Road) remain tightly closed, guarded by French Annamese and Chinese police for protection."

▲Citizens Already Affected　Since the strike of the machinery department employees, citizens in the French Concession have been affected. Activities such as installing water meters, electric meters, connecting electricity and water, and repairs have all been suspended. Public buses, trams, etc., in need of repair are unattended. Company meter reading and other tasks have been temporarily suspended. However, electricity generation and water supply are being maintained with difficulty by foreign workers.

▲Negotiations Continue Today　In order to quickly resolve the labor dispute at the French Water and Electricity Company, the municipal government sent Yang Shugeng and Ji Ji to negotiate with French Consul Mery. It is reported that they will continue to negotiate with the French Consul today (Monday). The Municipal Party Committee and the Social Affairs Bureau have advised the workers to wait patiently for a legal solution and to maintain order. The Strike Committee has accepted the advice and ordered its members to comply.

▲Labor Union Refutes Statement　The Chairman of the Strike Committee yesterday issued a rebuttal to Lu Guanhong's absurd statement, stating: "When the meeting was held on the 7th, a request was submitted to the party and government organs to send personnel to provide guidance and to have the picket line elected by the department meeting maintain order. There was absolutely no reason for non-members to infiltrate and disrupt the meeting. Lu Guanhong is colluding with the capitalists and selling out the interests of the workers. He actually made absurd remarks at the meeting and had his son Jinrong disrupt the meeting. Public sentiment was aroused, leading to his son being pulled away from his seat. Lu's gang then committed violence, resulting in the crowd injuring them. As for the confinement in a small room, representatives of the party and government organs witnessed it on the spot, leaving no room for denial." (The rest is omitted)

▲The Labor Union Presents Conditions　The Second District Water and Electricity Industry Union submitted a document to the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau yesterday, stating: "Regarding the submission of twelve conditions, we earnestly request that they be filed for record and that you promptly negotiate with the capitalists, ordering them to accept them. We have repeatedly submitted documents to your bureau and the Municipal Party Committee for mediation, which are on file. Since the capitalists have not provided a clear statement and have dismissed employees, causing public outrage and forcing us to resort to strike, it is truly unavoidable. Therefore, on the 8th, the general assembly of the masses, due to the stubbornness of the capitalists and driven by the need for food and clothing, has put forward the most basic and appropriate conditions. Including the previous case, there are a total of twelve items, namely: (1) Rescue Xu Amei from prison. The method is to request the capitalists to prove that Xu is not a communist, pay his wages during his imprisonment, and the capitalists must compensate for all expenses incurred during his imprisonment, such as lawyer fees and medical expenses. Reinstate him after his release from prison. (2) Reinstate Zhu Along and the other twenty-one people, and provide back pay for the period of suspension. (3) Reinstate Shao Ziying. (4) Restore the union's regular expenses to the original amount of two hundred yuan. Due to high rent, increased property taxes, and all kinds of miscellaneous expenses for the salaries of union staff, we feel that the expenses are insufficient. Therefore, in addition to the original amount of two hundred yuan, an additional three hundred yuan should be added, that is, the regular expenses must be paid at five hundred yuan from now on. (5) Pay wages as usual during the strike. (6) The capitalists should dismiss Lu Guanhong to appease the employees. (7) Pay each employee a monthly housing allowance of six yuan. (8) Increase the salaries of all employees, large and small, by 15% at the end of the year. (9) Issue uniforms to all employees inside and outside the factory. (10) The capitalists should reinstate the old contract. (11) The capitalists are not allowed to hire White Russians. (12) Employees who do not take leave for one month should receive an additional four days' wages. All members of our union believe that the above items are not excessive demands and have been passed on the spot. We are submitting this document for your bureau's record. We believe that your bureau has always taken it as its mission to solve the suffering of the people and seek the interests of the workers, and especially spares no effort to lead and support the workers. Therefore, we are submitting this document, hoping that you will promptly negotiate with the capitalists according to the above requests to benefit the labor movement. We are awaiting your orders." (The document to the Municipal Party Committee is omitted)

French Water and Electricity Company 136

Chinese Employees Withdraw from the Labor Union

▲And Establish a Fellowship Association

Guowen News Agency reports: Chinese employees of the French Water and Electricity Company in this city suddenly withdrew from the labor union yesterday and established a separate employee fellowship association, announcing various reasons, which are recorded as follows:

▲Declaration of Establishment of the Fellowship Association　We, all Chinese employees of the French Electric Company, since joining the labor union, have been blindly following the command of a few workers and passively dragged into the vortex of repeated labor disputes, without any so-called genuine will or freedom to express our will. We have come to the point where we dare not disobey any proposal made by the workers, whether reasonable or not. Even if we disagree, we are immediately whipped and beaten. All of us employees have always adhered to the principle of "more things done, more things go wrong". We have endured and followed, with our hearts and wishes far apart. We dare not hold any dissenting opinions, and we have no active or obvious actions. Through repeated endurance, our own will and freedom have been almost completely deprived by a few clamorous individuals. After thinking repeatedly, we have bravely risen up to organize a purely employee fellowship association to protect the genuine interests of all of us Chinese employees and to express our true will, so that we will not blindly follow and passively attach ourselves. As for the reasonable actions of our fellow workers, we will still adhere to our original intention and sympathize with and assist them. We hereby declare.

▲Letter to the Labor Union Declaring Withdrawal　Dear Sirs, we joined the labor union in July of the 19th year of the Republic of China (1930), originally to assist our fellow workers, based entirely on reasonable mutual assistance. In all the labor-management disputes that have arisen in the past, we have always sympathized with and cooperated with the workers. Although we dare not claim to have made contributions, we believe we can be acquitted of any wrongdoing towards our fellow workers. However, what we regret is that we feel that our positions and the workers' positions are slightly different, and our views are slightly different. Taking the current turmoil as an example, we also feel that the steps taken by the workers are slightly inappropriate. We believe that when the incident first occurred, we could have selected capable representatives to discuss the matter with the capitalists at length, or given the capitalists a reasonable deadline to respond within a longer period of time. As for strike actions, we should have reserved them as a last resort. For example, if two people have a dispute, how can they rashly resort to force? Is it not likely to lead to a stalemate? The current strike did not have the full consent of everyone beforehand. On the morning of the 7th, the day of the work stoppage, when the six representatives reported back, a large number of colleagues proposed to resume work first in the afternoon and wait for the representatives to continue negotiating with the capitalists until the 10th of this month. After all, the right to strike or not is in our hands. Even if we return to work now, if the capitalists do not give a reasonable reply by the deadline, we can start a strike again. Would this not have been a viable option? This proposal was not rejected on the spot. How can it be said that everyone agreed to it? Now that things are like this, what is done cannot be undone. What we should pay the most attention to is how to resolve the incident. After thinking repeatedly, we have the following requests: We are withdrawing from the labor union from today onwards. There are other reasons and statements, which will be published in the newspapers. Please pay attention. After this, although we are completely detached from the labor union, we can still actively assist in the event of sympathetic incidents, and even take concerted action. Not only that, now that we have withdrawn from the labor union, then in the future, whenever there are labor-management issues, whether they concern the workers or the employees, we can come forward as third parties to mediate. We feel that there is more room for maneuver in everything. Is this not the case? Furthermore, we are now establishing an association, and we will be conducting mediation of this dispute soon. If the workers as a whole or individuals have any opinions, please do not hesitate to share them with us, so that we can adopt them. This is what we hope for most.

▲Notice of Withdrawal from the Labor Union　We hereby respectfully inform you that the strike turmoil that occurred in the company this time was not with the prior consent of everyone, nor did it adopt the views of the majority after the event. It was entirely manipulated by a small number of people, fabricating public opinion and arbitrarily playing around. Even if someone disagreed, they were immediately beaten. There have been countless instances of beatings and scoldings in the past. This kind of behavior is something that all of us colleagues cannot condone. Whenever meetings are held, the venue is completely controlled by a few radical elements, making our employees silent and unable to express their will freely. This has led to all of us Chinese employees having no status in the labor union, except for bearing various nominal responsibilities. If it is said to be a work stoppage, then we can only follow suit. If it is said to be a strike, then we can only follow suit. If we are slightly more moderate or propose other ideas, we will immediately be whipped and beaten, or we will be labeled as capitalist running dogs and accused of sabotaging the labor movement. Repeatedly, all proposals made at meetings are radical, because no one dares to remain moderate anymore. If this continues, not only will our personal freedom and will be completely deprived, but we will inevitably be abandoned by society and suffer unjust grievances for a long time. Now, in addition to sending a letter to the labor union declaring our withdrawal, we are publishing this notice in the newspaper. Furthermore, our Chinese employees joined the labor union originally in July of the 19th year of the Republic of China (1930), originally to assist our fellow workers, based entirely on reasonable mutual assistance. We have also mediated labor-management disputes several times in the past, and we have always sympathized with and cooperated with the workers. Who knew that in recent years, we have become obligated and passive participants in the French Electric Company's labor disputes? Whenever the workers take any action, whether it is reasonable or not, we must follow suit, otherwise disaster will strike. Such official acquiescence is contrary to our will. If we do not withdraw quickly, where will we end up? We hereby declare the above and ask for the understanding of all sectors of society.

Chu Minyi Holds Sino-Belgian Meetings 137

Mr. Chu Minyi came to Shanghai this time to hold two important Sino-Belgian meetings: (1) the Sino-Belgian Health Construction Fund Committee, and (2) the Sino-Belgian Education and Culture Fund Committee. Both committees are affiliated with the Chinese delegation of the Sino-Belgian Boxer Indemnity Committee. Mr. Chu is the chairman of the congress. After arriving in Shanghai the day before yesterday, he convened the Sino-Belgian Health Construction Fund Committee at 2:00 PM. Commissioners Li Shizeng, Zeng Zongjian, Cai Hong, Song Wusheng, and Ge Chengzhi attended the meeting and resolved to establish a Sino-Belgian Venereal Disease Hospital. The committee will allocate 2,000 yuan per month from the fund to subsidize it. Chu Minyi and Zeng Zongjian were designated as commissioners in charge of cultural funds, and the list of commissioners will be submitted to the Executive Yuan for record. After the meeting, Mr. Chu took the evening train back to Beijing that night.

Zhu Jiqing 138

Speech ("How to Save China")

▲At the invitation of the Chaozhou Fellow Provincial Association's Four Educations National Salvation Corps, at 2:00 PM the day before yesterday, the Chaozhou Shanghai Fellow Provincial Association's Four Educations National Salvation Corps specially invited Mr. Zhu Jiqing, a member of the Central Committee who had just arrived in Shanghai from the Northeast, to give a speech. More than 300 members attended the meeting. First, Chairman Zheng Zhengqiu gave an introductory speech, stating: "Mr. Zhu is a person who has contributed to the Republic of China. Whether in or out of office, he has never forgotten the revolution. He has a spirit of perseverance and a bright and great personality. He has returned from the Northeast this time and is familiar with the situation. This association has specially invited him to speak on the current situation and to guide the direction of national salvation. The significance of today's meeting is extremely important. We hope that everyone will earnestly strive and work hard according to Mr. Zhu's guidance." Next, Mr. Zhu Jiqing gave a speech entitled "How to Save China." (The long speech will be recorded separately) Next, Mr. Liu Houwu described the beginning and end of Mr. Zhu's trip to the Northeast to lead the people in their struggle, as well as his mission in Shanghai this time. Finally, the chairman delivered a speech of encouragement and dismissal. The following is Zhu Jiqing's speech:

The Chaozhou Shanghai Fellow Provincial Association has always made great contributions to all aspects of the country and society. This time, it has organized the Four Educations National Salvation Corps to prepare for national salvation by cultivating the mind and body. Its profound intention is truly worthy of admiration. Three months ago, I went outside the customs to guide armed civilians in national salvation work. I saw the broken mountains and rivers and the tyrannical behavior of the enemy with my own eyes. I was already filled with infinite grief and indignation in my heart. This time, I returned to Beijing and Shanghai for business and had the opportunity to discuss the issue of national salvation with you. I couldn't help but feel happy again. This is because the compatriots outside the customs are struggling hard there for national salvation and are looking forward to reinforcements. You are here preparing for national salvation. Some people are fighting in the front, and some people are preparing in the rear. In this way, responding to each other from the front and rear and working together, there will definitely be a day when the lost land of the Northeast will be recovered, and the Chinese nation will not be destroyed. Isn't this a joyful thing? Speaking of the meaning of the two words "national salvation," it goes without saying that we know that the country is in danger and we must try to save it. There are many dangers in China now, but the most important one is the Northeast issue. The Northeast is to China as the brain and spinal cord are to the human body. If a person loses the brain and spinal cord, then that person will surely die. If China loses the Northeast, then China will surely be destroyed. Not to mention Japan's continental policy, which is not only to occupy the Northeast but also to annex the whole of China. Judging from the historical facts, China's external troubles since ancient times have all come from the north, such as the Five Barbarian Invasions and the Yuan and Qing dynasties' entry into the Central Plains. Therefore, if we want to save China, we must first save the Northeast. If we can save the Northeast, we can preserve China. Then, how exactly should we save the Northeast? I think you all know that the three words "non-resistance" have already created a big mistake, and expecting international sanctions is like a mirage, with no practical effect. In this situation, apart from using the strength of the nation itself to engage in long-term resistance, we cannot solely blame the government authorities or other aspects. Instead, all citizens must take responsibility. As the ancients said, "The rise and fall of a country is the responsibility of every individual." Since we, as citizens, cannot shirk our responsibility for the fall of the Northeast, we, as citizens, are of course duty-bound to recover the Northeast in the future. Moreover, the main reason for the arrival of national disasters lies in the fact that politics is not enlightened, and the main reason for the lack of enlightenment in politics lies in the absence of democratic forces. Therefore, if we want to fundamentally eliminate external troubles, we must make every effort to exert democratic forces, which will have a practical effect. The point of gathering armed civilians and organizing the Northeast National Salvation Army outside the customs is this. At the beginning of the September 18th Incident, the Japanese army occupied the lands of Liaoning and Jilin provinces within twenty-four hours. Afterwards, it encountered resistance from the people everywhere. It has been nine months now, and not only has it not been able to govern peacefully, but it is also exhausted. This shows how powerful the civilian armed forces are. At the same time, it is even more evident that only civilian armed forces can maintain the glory of the nation. As I just said, there is only one way to save the Northeast, and that is long-term resistance. When it comes to long-term resistance, there must be preparation for long-term resistance. However, this so-called preparation does not mean waiting for several or tens of years before resisting. It means resisting while preparing. Such a two-pronged approach, advancing simultaneously, being unyielding, and persisting to the end, then with China's vast land, large population, and abundant resources, I believe that it will be able to achieve final victory. On the other hand, if we wait for several or tens of years before resisting, then Japan, during those several or tens of years, can govern peacefully and create a deeply rooted situation. At that time, even if we want to resist, it will be too late, and I am afraid that it will not be easy to do. At present, the compatriots in the Northeast are fighting the enemy to the death in the front, so that Japan cannot get a chance to govern peacefully. As for whether they can persist to the end, it all depends on whether the compatriots in the rear can actively work hard to prepare and help them. Preparation can be divided into material and spiritual aspects. Material creation and invention depend on the role of the spirit, but for the spirit to play a role, it must also rely on the supply of materials. Just look at the anti-Japanese Northeast armed civilians. Their national spirit can be said to be fully expressed, but without material support, they cannot kill the enemy empty-handed. In this way, the spirit and matter are interdependent and cannot be separated. The name of your group is the Four Educations National Salvation Corps, and the purpose of your group is to cultivate the mind and body to prepare for national salvation. The so-called four educations are physical education, moral education, intellectual education, and social education. Physical education is to cultivate a healthy body, moral education is to cultivate noble morals, intellectual education is to cultivate rich knowledge, and social education is to cultivate the ability to work in groups. In other words, social education is to be sincerely united. You must use a healthy body, noble morals, rich knowledge, and sincere unity to save the country. There are more than 400 million people in China, including many with healthy bodies, noble morals, and rich knowledge. Unfortunately, they cannot be sincerely united, like a heap of loose sand, allowing national disasters to erupt uncontrollably. Therefore, in my opinion, you should put special effort into the item of social education and not only cultivate the mind and body but also engage in material invention or creation while cultivating the mind and body. Only in this way can you be considered a perfect preparation for national salvation. As for the situation in the Northeast, I have repeatedly published it in the newspapers in recent days and do not need to repeat it in detail. Now, I can only briefly summarize the situation in all aspects and say a few words. The Japanese army, having occupied our territory in the Northeast, destroyed our sovereignty and is still using various means of oppression to drive out our people, intending to completely turn the three northeastern provinces into Japanese colonies in name and in fact, and then annex the whole of China to implement its so-called continental policy. This is something that the people of the country should pay close attention to at all times. Although Japan has such sinister plans, it has been nine months since the September 18th Incident, and it has not had a chance to govern peacefully. Moreover, it has suffered several great difficulties. First, the Japanese army can only be stationed in various cities and along the railway lines and dare not leave ten or twenty miles away easily. If they leave, they are often wiped out by armed civilians. Second, since the incident, our country has suffered extreme trampling, and Japan has also suffered extreme losses. The headquarters of the Japanese invasion of the Northeast used to have an average annual income of 200 million Japanese yen, and the net profit was no less than 30 million Japanese yen. However, from April 1, 1932, to March 31, 1933, not only was there no profit to speak of, but there was also a loss of more than 3.4 million yuan. The South Manchuria Railway Company is still like this, and the rest can be imagined. Third, the Japanese government is suffering from economic downturn and heavy military spending, and its finances are already unsustainable. By the end of April, the shortfall in their national treasury's income had reached more than 100 million yuan. If this continues, how can they bear it? Moreover, Japan's occupation of the Northeast is not the will of all their citizens, but the arbitrary action of the warlords. In a certain sense, it is also a struggle between Japanese military power and civil rights. The Japanese civil rights movement has been growing stronger year by year. In order to maintain their special ruling position, the warlords do not hesitate to waste manpower and money, using the pretext of developing the country's power to occupy our Northeast and suppress our civil rights movement. This behavior of the Japanese warlords is tantamount to digging a grave for their country and throwing themselves on the road to decline. However, the length of their decline and the amount of sacrifice we suffer all depend on how hard our Chinese nation struggles. I sincerely hope that you will all become national salvation heroes, recover the Northeast, and preserve the whole of China.

Haining Compatriots Telegraph Zhejiang Officials to Request Suspension of Tax Collection

Haining compatriots in Shanghai telegraphed the Chairman of the Zhejiang Provincial Government, the Director of the Finance Department, and the Magistrate of Haining County yesterday, saying:

Chairman Lu of the Hangzhou Provincial Government, Director Zhou of the Finance Department, and Magistrate Wang Jun of Haining County, we acknowledge receipt. Haining County has had consecutive poor harvests in recent years. This spring, the silkworm crop failed and the cocoon prices were low. The people's savings are already exhausted, and their livelihoods have been cut off. Starvation and suicide are unfortunately common. Desperate risks have led to a collective grain-snatching trend. If it continues to spread, it will be difficult to control. The county government is still collecting taxes at this time, which further provokes the anger of the people. Therefore, we urgently telegraph your seat, requesting you to quickly allocate large sums of money to provide urgent relief to save the dying people. At the same time, immediately telegraph the county government to suspend tax collection and withdraw the special tax collection officers, so as to prolong their lives and eliminate hidden dangers. We are deeply grateful.

From the Ningbo Haichang Public Association and the Haining Relief Donation Association, Xu Guangpu and others bow.

National Postal Workers' Congress Postponed ▲ Representatives Pushed to Explain to the Central Government

The National Postal Workers' Union originally scheduled its annual congress for the 15th of this month in Shanghai, and had notified representatives from various regions to attend. However, it subsequently received a telegram from the central government, ordering the Ministry of Communications to stop it. The postal workers believe that the central government may not have understood the inside story, so they have specially sent representatives to Beijing to explain to the central government to avoid misunderstandings. The congress will be postponed to next month.

Chu Minyi Feasts Lin Baek

Government Legal Advisor Lin Baek arrived in Shanghai from Europe. Member of the Central Committee, Mr. Chu Minyi, held a banquet at his private residence the day before yesterday to welcome Mr. Lin. This was reported in yesterday's newspaper. According to Mr. Chu, Mr. Lin Baek once served as the Legal Advisor to the Premier and has traveled extensively to various countries, engaging in international propaganda for our party, which has been quite diligent. I and Mr. Lin are also old acquaintances. This time he came to China, so I invited friends in Shanghai to welcome him. The banquet was entirely social in nature and did not discuss any official business. However, when Mr. Lin came to China two years ago, he advocated a plan for a raw silver loan and suggested it to our government. Because there was no concrete plan, it was not implemented. Now, after more than a year, Mr. Lin has come to China again. It is still difficult to predict whether the plan he is discussing will be adopted by the central government.

Minhang Two Associations Send Telegram to Ministry of Finance

The Minhang Soy Sauce, Wine, Tobacco and Paper Industry Associations telegraphed the Ministry of Finance in Nanjing, saying:

Urgent, to the Ministry of Finance in Nanjing, we acknowledge receipt. Both the Ministry of Finance and the provincial government have issued announcements regarding the tobacco and alcohol license tax in Jiangsu Province. Merchants and citizens believe that paying taxes is an obligation that must be fulfilled. Whether it is managed by the Ministry or the province, it should be paid. It is only because the government orders are inconsistent and there is nothing to follow. If this license tax is still managed by the Ministry, the provincial government should be consulted to immediately abolish the established tax collection bureaus. If the provincial government is allowed to manage it on its own, the affiliated collection agencies should be ordered to close as soon as possible. Only then will merchants and citizens have something to follow.

Shanghai County Minhang Soy Sauce and Wine Industry Association, Tobacco and Paper Industry Association bow.

Hawkers Traveling to France Detained ▲ Passports Believed to be Forged ▲ Wrongfully Detained, Released with Proof

The French Consulate General in Shanghai previously received a telegram from Saigon, intercepting sixteen hawker passports traveling from Shanghai to France, all of which were forged. The sixteen hawkers were detained. One of them, in extreme anger, assaulted someone and was seriously injured. He is being treated in Saigon and will be deported after he recovers. The remaining fifteen detainees were sent to Shanghai by the Messageries Maritimes (霞道斯) mail ship and transferred to the Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau for interrogation. After questioning by the Third Section of the Bureau, each of the hawkers stated that these passports were purchased from the Gonghechang Exchange Shop in Nanshi for more than 300 yuan, including the ship ticket. Detectives were immediately dispatched to Gonghechang for arrest, but the shop owners had already fled in fear of punishment. Only three suspects were taken into custody, and Gonghechang was sealed. It is now heard that these passports are not forged and were indeed issued by the Guangzhou Municipal Public Security Bureau. After the Guangzhou Municipal Public Security Bureau sent a letter to the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau to provide proof, the three suspects were released.

Russian Beggar's Corpse to be Examined Today

The suspicious death of Russian beggar Georgy Latygin, who died in the Second Special District Court Detention Center, has caused a stir in society and attracted attention from Chinese and foreigners. The court has notified the Tongren Fuyuan Funeral Home to transport the coffin to Shanghai for examination to clarify the truth. The director of the Tongren Fuyuan Funeral Home, Mr. Qin Shounong, for the sake of prudence, specially sent two staff members and four laborers to the Nanshi Life Saving Bureau yesterday morning to borrow a rescue boat to transport the coffin. Due to the small tide period and the long distance, fearing that they would not be able to arrive in time and miss the formalities, they hired a small tugboat to tow it to the Tangwan Cemetery. They exhumed the coffin, verified the number, affixed a strip of paper, and loaded it onto the original boat for transportation to Shanghai. It is expected to arrive at the port at 8 AM this morning. An official letter will be sent to the Second Special District Court to be forwarded to the Shanghai Municipal Council morgue for examination.

Public Security Seventh District Uncovers Theft and Sale of Fort Machinery

Around 1 PM the day before yesterday, the Public Security Seventh District of Wusong received a tip-off that someone was stealing and selling important machinery from the Lion Grove Fort and planning to secretly transport it out of Songkou by boat. After receiving the report, the Seventh District, despite the heavy rain, immediately dispatched District Officer Yin Gongtian, along with detectives Wang Yao, Fan Yunhai, Zhao Huairen, and Li Jinqing, and several police officers, to secretly guard the entrance of the Yunzaobang Sitang. Anticipating that the boat would pass through here to leave the port, they waited until dawn yesterday when they saw a boat slowly approaching. District Officer Yin immediately ordered the detectives to approach and order the boat to shore for inspection. They found it fully loaded with artillery machinery, gun carriages, shell casings, and other valuable items. The boatmen and five others were arrested on the spot. They claimed that the machinery and other items were purchased from Wang Adong near the Lion Grove Fort. Wang Yao and others were dispatched to Wang Adong's house for a search, but Wang had already fled upon hearing the news. Only Wang's uncle, Wang Xingqing, was taken into custody. Artillery parts, gun carriage copper parts, and other goods such as barracks lumber were found in Wang's house. A coastal searchlight engine from the fortress was also seized from Fei Songhe's house behind Wang's house (Fei was also on the run). Because the engine was heavy, it was assigned to the police station for safekeeping. Two more suspects were subsequently apprehended near the Lion Grove Fort and taken into custody. Under the strict interrogation of District Chief Li, the suspects confessed that one was Xu Xiaochang, 30 years old, from Yancheng, residing in a thatched shed in Zhangjiabang, Yangshupu, Shanghai; one was Ma Chaoji, 55 years old, from Zhenjiang, residing on Gongping Road, Shanghai; one was Zhou Heyuan, 36 years old, from Zhenjiang, residing on Gongping Road, Shanghai; one was Yao Xinchang, 25 years old, from Gaoyou (boatman); and one was Wu Wanyuan, 50 years old, from Xinghua (boatman). The suspects Guo Shiying and Jin Weiqing were scrap dealers. Wang Xingqing was a local resident, 67 years old. Xu Xiaochang confessed that on the 8th of this month, he and Zhou Heyuan, Ma Chaoji, Chen Xinfu, and others purchased and received [items] from Wang Adong in Lion Grove Fort and sought leniency. The district chief verified the confessions. Considering the severity of the crime of colluding to steal fortress artillery parts, he submitted a report to the General Bureau. The suspects Guo Shiying and Jin Weiqing were released, and Wang Xingqing was released on bail. At the same time, he strictly ordered the subordinates and the Seventh Security Company to apprehend the fugitives Wang Adong and Fei Songhe and bring them to justice for interrogation.

July 14th is the anniversary of the establishment of the French Republic. The Western and Chinese members of the fire brigade are also rushing to tie up pine and cypress lanterns on the fire trucks in preparation for participating in the lantern parade competition.

The robbers, Zhang Xingfu, Jin Heshang, and Gao Heshang from Ningbo, armed and organized a gang to rob Mrs. Luo Wang from Guangdong at No. 1133, East Xihua De Road for clothing worth 738 yuan around noon on the 24th of last month. They fled to the house at No. 159, Aerok Road, where Chinese Detective Cai Zhitian and Detective Qi Mengqing of the Huishan Police Station learned of the situation. They secretly went together with Western detectives to arrest the three robbers, along with the woman Jin Cai, and took them all into the police station. They were sent to the Fourth Criminal Court of the First Special District Court the day before yesterday. The police lawyer Zhang Tianyin said that the defendants had admitted their guilt in the police station. Because the accomplices had not yet been caught, he requested an extension. He presented the stolen goods for inspection. Then the victim Luo Wang said that there were five robbers at the time. They entered from the back door. One robber asked if there was a Gu family in her house. She replied no. The defendant Gao Heshang said, "Please help," and took out a pistol to warn them not to make a sound. Then they went upstairs and rummaged through the boxes and cabinets, and began to search and rob. They fled from the back door with a hoot. She pointed out that the defendant Jin Heshang had a towel wrapped around his face at the time and could not see clearly. The clothes presented in the case were indeed the original stolen goods. According to Zhang Xing's confession, he did not enter the house. Xiaoshaoxing said that the victim's house had a large amount of opium and asked him to go and rob it. The rest of the confession was evasive. Jin Heshang confessed that there were five people who went at that time. He did not know about the meals and the sporadic expenses. Zhang Xingfu and Gao Heshang did go together, but he did not wrap a towel around his face and did not enter the house, only standing guard at the back door. Gao Heshang confessed that he only knew Jin Heshang for three days. Xiaoshaoxing was the one who initiated the matter. He denied threatening Luo Wang with a gun. Jin Cai confessed that she was the wife of * Heshang. Zhang Xingfu asked her to pawn the clothes and took * with him. She did not enter the house. Judge Shen ordered them to be taken back to prison separately for further investigation.

Mogan Mountain Guide Published

Mogan Mountain is a resort for escaping the summer heat. The mountains are covered with bamboo, which is cool and pleasant. The highest temperature has never exceeded 86 degrees. In recent years, Chinese and Westerners have flocked to the mountain for summer vacation. The China Travel Service has always been dedicated to serving the society. In addition to establishing a summer office in the mountain with the Shanghai Bank, it recently compiled and printed a Mogan Mountain Guide, because tourists climbing the mountain suffer from the lack of a practical book. The content is rich and very interesting. It is divided into more than ten categories, including overview, area, scenic spots, hotels, transportation, public utilities, agencies, itinerary, arts and culture, and appendices. There are dozens of illustrations. The entire book has more than 100 pages, printed on high quality paper. The cover is signed by Mr. Huang Yingbai and printed with a light green bamboo forest landscape, which is very exquisite. The company mainly promotes travel, not for profit from selling books. Each copy is only sold for half the cost, 20 cents. It is on sale from today. Those who want to visit Mogan Mountain in this hot summer should have a copy.

It was publicly decided: (A) To issue a warning to the professors and scholars hired by Wang Jingwei to study diplomacy, urging them to follow their conscience and adhere to the right path. (B) To severely criticize the claims of Hu Shi et al. (C) Regarding the fundamental foreign policy, to ask the diplomatic experts of the Work Plan Promotion Committee to discuss it and submit it to the Standing Committee for consideration and action. (5) The Peiping representatives proposed raising funds to aid the Northeast Volunteer Army. It was publicly decided to consult the Northeast Volunteer Army Support Association to actively proceed. (6) The D District Japanese troops have not yet withdrawn. It was publicly decided to telegraph the government to send troops to expel them from the country. The meeting adjourned at 6 PM.

National Salvation Propaganda Week, Day Six 142

▲ Held at Shanghai Girls' High School Yesterday

▲ Closing Ceremony at West Gate Today

Yesterday was the sixth day of the Shanghai various groups' National Salvation United Association's National Salvation Propaganda Week in the Little West Gate area of the city. The location was Shanghai Girls' High School in the West Gate area. The weather yesterday was extremely hot, and people were sweating profusely, but the enthusiasm of the audience increased with the weather. It was estimated that more than 600 people participated. The order of the venue was maintained by the Shanghai Middle School Boy Scouts, who also distributed publications. The Chairman was Chen Ya'fu, the Secretary was Jiang Daiqing, the Entertainment Director was Chen Peide, the Speech Chairman was Zhang Tianbai, the Stage Director was Xu Gongmei, the Reception Director was Wu Zhijian, the Front Stage Director was Yu Zhenhui, the General Manager was Song An, the Staff Member was Hu Yueqin, and the Receptionists were Pan Qiwen, Wu Yingxue, and Zhang Hequn. The Master of Ceremonies was Guo Xiuyan. The Chairman's report briefly stated: "We are Chinese, we want to save China, we want to unite as one, work together, oppose internal wars, urge the government to send troops to recover lost territory, and at the same time, the people must strengthen national power and prepare for war with the enemy. This is not a matter for one person, it is the key to the survival of the entire nation, so everyone should take on the national responsibility and prepare to be soldiers in the national war in military and economic terms. Those of you who are here today probably already understand this meaning, and I hope you will pass this meaning on to every compatriot, then your trip here will not be in vain, and this event of ours will not be in vain." Zhang Tianbai then gave a speech, followed by the entertainment performance. The event has been held for a week, and today is the last day. The closing ceremony will be held today at the Little West Gate Children's Propaganda Group, and various entertainment programs will participate to create a final grand gathering.
